*** New Entry ***
Entry	Entry key: 123
time:	14/08/02 03:51:47
name:	Capture 107
comments:	The program abruptly closed itself during capture 106. I've seen this behaviour before when running a second python program while CRISTAL is running (as was the case now, was plotting saturation curves). It seems that, as soon as CRISTAL encounters an error (which it did, I chose a 0 bin width, so it throws a division error), it just force-shutdowns itself rather than just throw an error and continue. This has happened a few times already when running a second python script. Strange. 

So, note: do not run other python scripts while CRISTAL is running.
#End of comment
people:	Ruben

We are now optimizing the laser ion rate.
